Family Trace\\n\\n### 1. Core Joda-Beans Domain Classes (modules/product/)\\n\\nThe four core domain classes form the primary type hierarchy for FX vanilla options:\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOption** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOption.java): The core vanilla FX option product class annotated with @BeanDefinition. It implements FxOptionProduct and Resolvable<ResolvedFxVanillaOption>. Contains properties for longShort, expiryDate, expiryTime, expiryZone, and underlying FxSingle.\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionTrade** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTrade.java): A trade wrapper around FxVanillaOption that implements FxOptionTrade and ResolvableTrade<ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade>. Contains TradeInfo, product, and premium (AdjustablePayment).\\n\\n- **ResolvedFxVanillaOption** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOption.java): The resolved form of FxVanillaOption for pricing. Implements ResolvedProduct. Contains longShort, expiry (ZonedDateTime), and underlying (ResolvedFxSingle).\\n\\n- **ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade.java): The resolved form of FxVanillaOptionTrade. Implements ResolvedTrade. Contains TradeInfo, product (ResolvedFxVanillaOption), and premium (Payment).\\n\\n### 2. Pricer Classes (modules/pricer/)\\n\\nThe OpenGamma Strata codebase implements two main pricing models for FxVanillaOption, with separate product and trade pricers:\\n\\n**Black Model Pricers:**\\n- **BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java): Prices ResolvedFxVanillaOption using the Black (lognormal) model.\\n- **BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java): Prices ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade using Black volatilities.\\n\\n**Vanna-Volga Model Pricers:**\\n- **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java): Prices ResolvedFxVanillaOption using the Vanna-Volga model.\\n- **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java): Prices ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade using Vanna-Volga volatilities with smile.\\n\\n### 3. Measure Calculation Classes (modules/measure/)\\n\\nThe calculation layer wires pricers to the multi-scenario calculation engine:\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations.java): Multi-scenario calculation class holding references to BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer and VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer. Implements methods for presentValue, pv01, currencyExposure, delta, and vegaMarketQuoteBucketed.\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations.java): High-level calculations API that wraps FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations and provides convenience methods for pricing and risk measures.\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction.java): Implements CalculationFunction<FxVanillaOptionTrade> for integration with the Strata calculation engine. Maps measures (PresentValue, PV01, CurrencyExposure, etc.) to calculation methods.\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionMethod** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMethod.java): Enum (BLACK, VANNA_VOLGA) implementing CalculationParameter that allows users to specify which pricing method to use.\\n\\n### 4. Loader CSV Plugin (modules/loader/)\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin** (modules/loader/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/loader/csv/FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin.java): Implements TradeCsvParserPlugin and TradeCsvWriterPlugin<FxVanillaOptionTrade>. Handles reading and writing FX vanilla option trades in CSV format with fields for long/short, put/call, strike, expiry, currency pair, notional, and premium.\\n\\n### 5. Related Type: FxSingleBarrierOption (modules/product/)\\n\\n- **FxSingleBarrierOption** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxSingleBarrierOption.java): A related product that embeds FxVanillaOption as a dependency (underlyingOption property). Implements FxOptionProduct and Resolvable<ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption>. The barrier option wraps a vanilla option with barrier and rebate specifications.\\n\\n### Type Resolution Chain\\n\\nThe flow follows this pattern:\\n1. **Trade Creation**: User creates FxVanillaOptionTrade with FxVanillaOption and premium\\n2. **Resolution**: FxVanillaOptionTrade#resolve() converts to ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade with ResolvedFxVanillaOption\\n3. **Pricing**: BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer or VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer#presentValue() prices the resolved trade\\n4. **Calculations**: FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations orchestrates pricers for multiple measures\\n5. **Engine Integration**: FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction integrates with Strata's multi-scenario calculation engine\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Product vs Trade**: Clear separation between the financial product (option terms) and the trade (position and premium)\\n- **Unresolved vs Resolved**: Unresolved types (FxVanillaOption, FxVanillaOptionTrade) are used by business logic, while resolved types are bound to market data (calendars, rates) for pricing\\n- **Pricer Variants**: Multiple pricing models (Black, Vanna-Volga) available through same interface\\n- **Dual Abstraction Levels**: Product pricers handle pure valuation, trade pricers handle premium adjustments\\n- **CSV Loading**: Standardized CSV format for importing trades via TradeCsvLoaderTest integration\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3477,"cache_read_input_tokens":92548,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3477},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"9ae4936e-5beb-4469-8079-ad289f66d8c4","uuid":"fb979b5f-c1a1-4150-888b-46fc41d73411"}
